================================================================================
                               POLICY CONDITIONS
================================================================================

POLICY_FORM policy form                                             Policy No. YW700400

ITEM,STATE / CLASS
WC-0003,MA / 8742
CLASSIFICATION,PAYROLL / RATE
Outside salespersons,$70,826 / 0.18
PREMIUM,FORM
$127,WC 00 00 00 C 01 15

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**POLICY CONDITIONS**

This page applies to classification 8742 in MA as shown in the information page and classification schedule.

Estimated remuneration, class assignments, rates, and premium are subject to audit after the policy period.

The experience modification factor and schedule rating entry apply unless a state-specific endorsement provides otherwise.

Payroll records, job duties, certificates, and subcontractor information must be retained for rating verification.

No notice, inspection, or audit changes coverage unless an endorsement is issued and attached to the policy.

References to classification, remuneration, and rating basis include MA class code 8742 only for the state and operation shown in the information page.

Headings are included for ease of reading and do not alter statutory benefits, employers liability limits, audit rights, or state amendatory provisions.

If a state endorsement and a general condition address the same subject, the state-specific endorsement controls for the affected state.

The insured should retain payroll journals, tax filings, subcontractor certificates, job-duty records, and officer status records used to support the classification entries.

Classification summaries on one page do not replace the information page, payroll schedule, endorsement schedule, or premium audit statement.

A certificate, binder note, invoice, or producer correspondence item does not amend a payroll or class-code entry unless an endorsement is issued.

Final premium may require allocation of remuneration by state, governing class, officer status, overtime treatment, and subcontracted work records.

When a class code appears on multiple schedules, the state, item identifier, and effective date should be used to read the entries together.

**SECTION A - RECORDS AND AUDIT**

The insured must keep payroll journals, tax filings, job-duty records, and contract labor records for Outside salespersons assigned to class code 8742 in MA.

The remuneration entry of $70,826 is an estimate for rating purposes and may be revised after audit without changing the coverage afforded by the policy.

Separate records are required when an employee performs duties that may fall under more than one classification or more than one covered state.

If adequate records are not available, remuneration may be assigned to the highest rated applicable classification permitted by the rating rules.

**SECTION B - STATE AND CLASSIFICATION CONDITIONS**

State amendatory endorsements, statutory benefit provisions, and assigned-risk rules apply before any conflicting general condition in this policy packet.

A classification shown on a schedule is not a warranty that all operations at the insured location are limited to that class.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Blue Kettle Food Service, LLC                                        POLICY_FORM

**POLICY CONDITIONS**

This page applies to classification 8810 in CT as shown in the information page and classification schedule.

Headings are included for ease of reading and do not alter statutory benefits, employers liability limits, audit rights, or state amendatory provisions.

If a state endorsement and a general condition address the same subject, the state-specific endorsement controls for the affected state.

The insured should retain payroll journals, tax filings, subcontractor certificates, job-duty records, and officer status records used to support the classification entries.

Classification summaries on one page do not replace the information page, payroll schedule, endorsement schedule, or premium audit statement.

A certificate, binder note, invoice, or producer correspondence item does not amend a payroll or class-code entry unless an endorsement is issued.

Final premium may require allocation of remuneration by state, governing class, officer status, overtime treatment, and subcontracted work records.

When a class code appears on multiple schedules, the state, item identifier, and effective date should be used to read the entries together.

**SECTION A - RECORDS AND AUDIT**

### POLICY CONDITIONS

No notice, inspection, or audit changes coverage unless an endorsement is issued and attached to the policy.

References to classification, remuneration, and rating basis include MA class code 8742 only for the state and operation shown in the information page.

Headings are included for ease of reading and do not alter statutory benefits, employers liability limits, audit rights, or state amendatory provisions.

If a state endorsement and a general condition address the same subject, the state-specific endorsement controls for the affected state.

The insured should retain payroll journals, tax filings, subcontractor certificates, job-duty records, and officer status records used to support the classification entries.

Classification summaries on one page do not replace the information page, payroll schedule, endorsement schedule, or premium audit statement.

A certificate, binder note, invoice, or producer correspondence item does not amend a payroll or class-code entry unless an endorsement is issued.

Final premium may require allocation of remuneration by state, governing class, officer status, overtime treatment, and subcontracted work records.

When a class code appears on multiple schedules, the state, item identifier, and effective date should be used to read the entries together.


### SECTION A - RECORDS AND AUDIT

The insured must keep payroll journals, tax filings, job-duty records, and contract labor records for Outside salespersons assigned to class code 8742 in MA.

The remuneration entry of $158,051 is an estimate for rating purposes and may be revised after audit without changing the coverage afforded by the policy.

Separate records are required when an employee performs duties that may fall under more than one classification or more than one covered state.

If adequate records are not available, remuneration may be assigned to the highest rated applicable classification permitted by the rating rules.


### SECTION B - STATE AND CLASSIFICATION CONDITIONS

State amendatory endorsements, statutory benefit provisions, and assigned-risk rules apply before any conflicting general condition in this policy packet.

A classification shown on a schedule is not a warranty that all operations at the insured location are limited to that class.

Premium Audit and Accounting Conditions

YW700400
04/01/2026 - 04/01/2027

================================================================================
                           PREMIUM AUDIT AND ACCOUNTING CONDITIONS
================================================================================

BILLING policy form                                                      Policy No. YW700400

"ITEM","STATE / CLASS"
"WC-0025","CT / 8810"
"CLASSIFICATION","PAYROLL / RATE"
"Clerical office employees","$323,486 / 6.22"
"PREMIUM","FORM"
"$20,120","WC 00 03 13 07 23"

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**POLICY CONDITIONS**

This page applies to classification 8810 in CT as shown in the information page and classification schedule.

Estimated remuneration, class assignments, rates, and premium are subject to audit after the policy period.

The experience modification factor and schedule rating entry apply unless a state-specific endorsement provides otherwise.

Payroll records, job duties, certificates, and subcontractor information must be retained for rating verification.

No notice, inspection, or audit changes coverage unless an endorsement is issued and attached to the policy.

References to classification, remuneration, and rating basis include CT class code 8810 only for the state and operation shown in the information page.

Headings are included for ease of reading and do not alter statutory benefits, employers liability limits, audit rights, or state amendatory provisions.

If a state endorsement and a general condition address the same subject, the state-specific endorsement controls for the affected state.

The insured should retain payroll journals, tax filings, subcontractor certificates, job-duty records, and officer status records used to support the classification entries.

Classification summaries on one page do not replace the information page, payroll schedule, endorsement schedule, or premium audit statement.

A certificate, binder note, invoice, or producer correspondence item does not amend a payroll or class-code entry unless an endorsement is issued.

Final premium may require allocation of remuneration by state, governing class, officer status, overtime treatment, and subcontracted work records.

When a class code appears on multiple schedules, the state, item identifier, and effective date should be used to read the entries together.

**SECTION A - RECORDS AND AUDIT**

The insured must keep payroll journals, tax filings, job-duty records, and contract labor records for Clerical office employees assigned to class code 8810 in CT.

The remuneration entry of $323,486 is an estimate for rating purposes and may be revised after audit without changing the coverage afforded by the policy.

Separate records are required when an employee performs duties that may fall under more than one classification or more than one covered state.

If adequate records are not available, remuneration may be assigned to the highest rated applicable classification permitted by the rating rules.

**SECTION B - STATE AND CLASSIFICATION CONDITIONS**

State amendatory endorsements, statutory benefit provisions, and assigned-risk rules apply before any conflicting general condition in this policy packet.

A classification shown on a schedule is not a warranty that all operations at the insured location are limited to that class.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Blue Kettle Food Service, LLC                                                            BILLING

ITEM,STATE / CLASS

CLASSIFICATION,PAYROLL / RATE
Outside salespersons,$435,963 / 0.27
PREMIUM,FORM
$1,177,WC 00 00 00 C 04 21

***

**POLICY CONDITIONS**

This page applies to classification 8742 in MA as shown in the information page and classification schedule.

Estimated remuneration, class assignments, rates, and premium are subject to audit after the policy period.

The experience modification factor and schedule rating entry apply unless a state-specific endorsement provides otherwise.

Payroll records, job duties, certificates, and subcontractor information must be retained for rating verification.

No notice, inspection, or audit changes coverage unless an endorsement is issued and attached to the policy.

References to classification, remuneration, and rating basis include MA class code 8742 only for the state and operation shown in the information page.

Headings are included for ease of reading and do not alter statutory benefits, employers liability limits, audit rights, or state amendatory provisions.

If a state endorsement and a general condition address the same subject, the state-specific endorsement controls for the affected state.

The insured should retain payroll journals, tax filings, subcontractor certificates, job-duty records, and officer status records used to support the classification entries.

Classification summaries on one page do not replace the information page, payroll schedule, endorsement schedule, or premium audit statement.

A certificate, binder note, invoice, or producer correspondence item does not amend a payroll or class-code entry unless an endorsement is issued.

Final premium may require allocation of remuneration by state, governing class, officer status, overtime treatment, and subcontracted work records.

When a class code appears on multiple schedules, the state, item identifier, and effective date should be used to read the entries together.

**SECTION A - RECORDS AND AUDIT**

The insured must keep payroll journals, tax filings, job-duty records, and contract labor records for Outside salespersons assigned to class code 8742 in MA.

The remuneration entry of $435,963 is an estimate for rating purposes and may be revised after audit without changing the coverage afforded by the policy.

Separate records are required when an employee performs duties that may fall under more than one classification or more than one covered state.

If adequate records are not available, remuneration may be assigned to the highest rated applicable classification permitted by the rating rules.

**SECTION B - STATE AND CLASSIFICATION CONDITIONS**

State amendatory endorsements, statutory benefit provisions, and assigned-risk rules apply before any conflicting general condition in this policy packet.

A classification shown on a schedule is not a warranty that all operations at the insured location are limited to that class.

***

Blue Kettle Food Service, LLC

NOTICE policy form                                                   Policy No. YW700400

"ITEM","STATE / CLASS"
"WC-0041","CT / 8810"
"CLASSIFICATION","PAYROLL / RATE"
"Clerical office employees","$502,147 / 1.15"
"PREMIUM","FORM"
"$5,774","WC 00 03 13 04 21"

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**POLICY CONDITIONS**

This page applies to classification 8810 in CT as shown in the information page and classification schedule.

Estimated remuneration, class assignments, rates, and premium are subject to audit after the policy period.

The experience modification factor and schedule rating entry apply unless a state-specific endorsement provides otherwise.

Payroll records, job duties, certificates, and subcontractor information must be retained for rating verification.

No notice, inspection, or audit changes coverage unless an endorsement is issued and attached to the policy.

References to classification, remuneration, and rating basis include CT class code 8810 only for the state and operation shown in the information page.

Headings are included for ease of reading and do not alter statutory benefits, employers liability limits, audit rights, or state amendatory provisions.

If a state endorsement and a general condition address the same subject, the state-specific endorsement controls for the affected state.

The insured should retain payroll journals, tax filings, subcontractor certificates, job-duty records, and officer status records used to support the classification entries.

Classification summaries on one page do not replace the information page, payroll schedule, endorsement schedule, or premium audit statement.

---

A certificate, binder note, invoice, or producer correspondence item does not amend a payroll or class-code entry unless an endorsement is issued.

Final premium may require allocation of remuneration by state, governing class, officer status, overtime treatment, and subcontracted work records.

When a class code appears on multiple schedules, the state, item identifier, and effective date should be used to read the entries together.

**SECTION A - RECORDS AND AUDIT**

The insured must keep payroll journals, tax filings, job-duty records, and contract labor records for Clerical office employees assigned to class code 8810 in CT.

The remuneration entry of $502,147 is an estimate for rating purposes and may be revised after audit without changing the coverage afforded by the policy.

Separate records are required when an employee performs duties that may fall under more than one classification or more than one covered state.

If adequate records are not available, remuneration may be assigned to the highest rated applicable classification permitted by the rating rules.

**SECTION B - STATE AND CLASSIFICATION CONDITIONS**

State amendatory endorsements, statutory benefit provisions, and assigned-risk rules apply before any conflicting general condition in this policy packet.

A classification shown on a schedule is not a warranty that all operations at the insured location are limited to that class.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Blue Kettle Food Service, LLC                                             NOTICE

# Premium Audit and Accounting Conditions

____________________________________________________________________________________________________
                               PREMIUM AUDIT AND ACCOUNTING CONDITIONS
____________________________________________________________________________________________________

BILLING policy form                                                              Policy No. YW700400

ITEM,STATE / CLASS
WC-0051,MA / 8742
CLASSIFICATION,PAYROLL / RATE
Outside salespersons,$622,528 / 0.74
PREMIUM,FORM
$4,606,WC 00 03 13 04 21

____________________________________________________________________________________________________

### POLICY CONDITIONS

This page applies to classification 8742 in MA as shown in the information page and classification schedule.

Estimated remuneration, class assignments, rates, and premium are subject to audit after the policy period.

The experience modification factor and schedule rating entry apply unless a state-specific endorsement provides otherwise.

Payroll records, job duties, certificates, and subcontractor information must be retained for rating verification.

No notice, inspection, or audit changes coverage unless an endorsement is issued and attached to the policy.

References to classification, remuneration, and rating basis include MA class code 8742 only for the state and operation shown in the information page.

Headings are included for ease of reading and do not alter statutory benefits, employers liability limits, audit rights, or state amendatory provisions.

If a state endorsement and a general condition address the same subject, the state-specific endorsement controls for the affected state.

The insured should retain payroll journals, tax filings, subcontractor certificates, job-duty records, and officer status records used to support the classification entries.

Classification summaries on one page do not replace the information page, payroll schedule, endorsement schedule, or premium audit statement.

---

A certificate, binder note, invoice, or producer correspondence item does not amend a payroll or class-code entry unless an endorsement is issued.

Final premium may require allocation of remuneration by state, governing class, officer status, overtime treatment, and subcontracted work records.

When a class code appears on multiple schedules, the state, item identifier, and effective date should be used to read the entries together.

### SECTION A - RECORDS AND AUDIT

The insured must keep payroll journals, tax filings, job-duty records, and contract labor records for Outside salespersons assigned to class code 8742 in MA.

The remuneration entry of $622,528 is an estimate for rating purposes and may be revised after audit without changing the coverage afforded by the policy.

Separate records are required when an employee performs duties that may fall under more than one classification or more than one covered state.

If adequate records are not available, remuneration may be assigned to the highest rated applicable classification permitted by the rating rules.

### SECTION B - STATE AND CLASSIFICATION CONDITIONS

State amendatory endorsements, statutory benefit provisions, and assigned-risk rules apply before any conflicting general condition in this policy packet.

A classification shown on a schedule is not a warranty that all operations at the insured location are limited to that class.

____________________________________________________________________________________________________

PREMIUM AUDIT AND ACCOUNTING CONDITIONS
================================================================================

BILLING policy form                                            Policy No. YW700400

ITEM,STATE / CLASS
WC-0001,CT / 8810
CLASSIFICATION,PAYROLL / RATE
Clerical office employees,"$45,136 / 0.42"
PREMIUM,FORM
$189,WC 00 00 01 A 07 23

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

POLICY CONDITIONS

This page applies to classification 8810 in CT as shown in the information page and classification schedule.

Estimated remuneration, class assignments, rates, and premium are subject to audit after the policy period.

The experience modification factor and schedule rating entry apply unless a state-specific endorsement provides otherwise.

Payroll records, job duties, certificates, and subcontractor information must be retained for rating verification.

No notice, inspection, or audit changes coverage unless an endorsement is issued and attached to the policy.

References to classification, remuneration, and rating basis include CT class code 8810 only for the state and operation shown in the information page.

Headings are included for ease of reading and do not alter statutory benefits, employers liability limits, audit rights, or state amendatory provisions.

If a state endorsement and a general condition address the same subject, the state-specific endorsement controls for the affected state.

The insured should retain payroll journals, tax filings, subcontractor certificates, job-duty records, and officer status records used to support the classification entries.

Classification summaries on one page do not replace the information page, payroll schedule, endorsement schedule, or premium audit statement.

A certificate, binder note, invoice, or producer correspondence item does not amend a payroll or class-code entry unless an endorsement is issued.

Final premium may require allocation of remuneration by state, governing class, officer status, overtime treatment, and subcontracted work records.

When a class code appears on multiple schedules, the state, item identifier, and effective date should be used to read the entries together.

SECTION A - RECORDS AND AUDIT

The insured must keep payroll journals, tax filings, job-duty records, and contract labor records for Clerical office employees assigned to class code 8810 in CT.

The remuneration entry of $45,136 is an estimate for rating purposes and may be revised after audit without changing the coverage afforded by the policy.

Separate records are required when an employee performs duties that may fall under more than one classification or more than one covered state.

If adequate records are not available, remuneration may be assigned to the highest rated applicable classification permitted by the rating rules.

SECTION B - STATE AND CLASSIFICATION CONDITIONS

State amendatory endorsements, statutory benefit provisions, and assigned-risk rules apply before any conflicting general condition in this policy packet.

A classification shown on a schedule is not a warranty that all operations at the insured location are limited to that class.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Blue Kettle Food Service, LLC                                            BILLING

PREMIUM,FORM
$6,651,WC 04 03 06 04 21

**POLICY CONDITIONS**

This page applies to classification 8017 in CT as shown in the information page and classification schedule.

Estimated remuneration, class assignments, rates, and premium are subject to audit after the policy period.

The experience modification factor and schedule rating entry apply unless a state-specific endorsement provides otherwise.

Payroll records, job duties, certificates, and subcontractor information must be retained for rating verification.

No notice, inspection, or audit changes coverage unless an endorsement is issued and attached to the policy.

References to classification, remuneration, and rating basis include CT class code 8017 only for the state and operation shown in the information page.

Headings are included for ease of reading and do not alter statutory benefits, employers liability limits, audit rights, or state amendatory provisions.

If a state endorsement and a general condition address the same subject, the state-specific endorsement controls for the affected state.

The insured should retain payroll journals, tax filings, subcontractor certificates, job-duty records, and officer status records used to support the classification entries.

Classification summaries on one page do not replace the information page, payroll schedule, endorsement schedule, or premium audit statement.

A certificate, binder note, invoice, or producer correspondence item does not amend a payroll or class-code entry unless an endorsement is issued.

Final premium may require allocation of remuneration by state, governing class, officer status, overtime treatment, and subcontracted work records.

When a class code appears on multiple schedules, the state, item identifier, and effective date should be used to read the entries together.

**SECTION A - RECORDS AND AUDIT**

The insured must keep payroll journals, tax filings, job-duty records, and contract labor records for Retail store - all employees assigned to class code 8017 in CT.

The remuneration entry of $152,897 is an estimate for rating purposes and may be revised after audit without changing the coverage afforded by the policy.

Separate records are required when an employee performs duties that may fall under more than one classification or more than one covered state.

If adequate records are not available, remuneration may be assigned to the highest rated applicable classification permitted by the rating rules.

**SECTION B - STATE AND CLASSIFICATION CONDITIONS**

State amendatory endorsements, statutory benefit provisions, and assigned-risk rules apply before any conflicting general condition in this policy packet.

A classification shown on a schedule is not a warranty that all operations at the insured location are limited to that class.

**POLICY CONDITIONS**

This page applies to classification 9082 in RI as shown in the information page and classification schedule.

Estimated remuneration, class assignments, rates, and premium are subject to audit after the policy period.

The experience modification factor and schedule rating entry apply unless a state-specific endorsement provides otherwise.

Payroll records, job duties, certificates, and subcontractor information must be retained for rating verification.

No notice, inspection, or audit changes coverage unless an endorsement is issued and attached to the policy.

References to classification, remuneration, and rating basis include RI class code 9082 only for the state and operation shown in the information page.

Headings are included for ease of reading and do not alter statutory benefits, employers liability limits, audit rights, or state amendatory provisions.

If a state endorsement and a general condition address the same subject, the state-specific endorsement controls for the affected state.

The insured should retain payroll journals, tax filings, subcontractor certificates, job-duty records, and officer status records used to support the classification entries.

Classification summaries on one page do not replace the information page, payroll schedule, endorsement schedule, or premium audit statement.

A certificate, binder note, invoice, or producer correspondence item does not amend a payroll or class-code entry unless an endorsement is issued.

Final premium may require allocation of remuneration by state, governing class, officer status, overtime treatment, and subcontracted work records.

When a class code appears on multiple schedules, the state, item identifier, and effective date should be used to read the entries together.

**SECTION A - RECORDS AND AUDIT**

The insured must keep payroll journals, tax filings, job-duty records, and contract labor records for Restaurant NOC assigned to class code 9082 in RI.

The remuneration entry of $277,752 is an estimate for rating purposes and may be revised after audit without changing the coverage afforded by the policy.

Separate records are required when an employee performs duties that may fall under more than one classification or more than one covered state.

If adequate records are not available, remuneration may be assigned to the highest rated applicable classification permitted by the rating rules.

**SECTION B - STATE AND CLASSIFICATION CONDITIONS**

State amendatory endorsements, statutory benefit provisions, and assigned-risk rules apply before any conflicting general condition in this policy packet.

A classification shown on a schedule is not a warranty that all operations at the insured location are limited to that class.

### POLICY CONDITIONS

POLICY_FORM policy form
Policy No. YW700400

ITEM,STATE / CLASS
WC-0032,VT / 5606
CLASSIFICATION,PAYROLL / RATE
Contractor executive supervisor,$404,635 / 4.35
PREMIUM,FORM
$17,601,WC 00 00 01 A 04 21

**POLICY CONDITIONS**

This page applies to classification 5606 in VT as shown in the information page and classification schedule.

Estimated remuneration, class assignments, rates, and premium are subject to audit after the policy period.

The experience modification factor and schedule rating entry apply unless a state-specific endorsement provides otherwise.

Payroll records, job duties, certificates, and subcontractor information must be retained for rating verification.

No notice, inspection, or audit changes coverage unless an endorsement is issued and attached to the policy.

References to classification, remuneration, and rating basis include VT class code 5606 only for the state and operation shown in the information page.

Headings are included for ease of reading and do not alter statutory benefits, employers liability limits, audit rights, or state amendatory provisions.

If a state endorsement and a general condition address the same subject, the state-specific endorsement controls for the affected state.

The insured should retain payroll journals, tax filings, subcontractor certificates, job-duty records, and officer status records used to support the classification entries.

Classification summaries on one page do not replace the information page, payroll schedule, endorsement schedule, or premium audit statement.

A certificate, binder note, invoice, or producer correspondence item does not amend a payroll or class-code entry unless an endorsement is issued.

Final premium may require allocation of remuneration by state, governing class, officer status, overtime treatment, and subcontracted work records.

When a class code appears on multiple schedules, the state, item identifier, and effective date should be used to read the entries together.

**SECTION A - RECORDS AND AUDIT**

The insured must keep payroll journals, tax filings, job-duty records, and contract labor records for Contractor executive supervisor assigned to class code 5606 in VT.

The remuneration entry of $404,635 is an estimate for rating purposes and may be revised after audit without changing the coverage afforded by the policy.

Separate records are required when an employee performs duties that may fall under more than one classification or more than one covered state.

If adequate records are not available, remuneration may be assigned to the highest rated applicable classification permitted by the rating rules.

**SECTION B - STATE AND CLASSIFICATION CONDITIONS**

State amendatory endorsements, statutory benefit provisions, and assigned-risk rules apply before any conflicting general condition in this policy packet.

A classification shown on a schedule is not a warranty that all operations at the insured location are limited to that class.

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
                                             **POLICY CHANGE ENDORSEMENT**

Endorsement No. WC-EN-016                                                                             Effective 04/01/2026

ITEM,STATE / CLASS
WC-0016,VT / 5606
CLASSIFICATION,PAYROLL / RATE
Contractor executive supervisor,$223,415 / 2.86
PREMIUM,FORM
$6,389,WC 00 00 01 A 04 21
ENDORSEMENT,EFFECTIVE DATE
WC-EN-016,04/01/2026
MATERIALITY,
Material,

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**POLICY CONDITIONS**

This page applies to classification 5606 in VT as shown in the information page and classification schedule.

Estimated remuneration, class assignments, rates, and premium are subject to audit after the policy period.

The experience modification factor and schedule rating entry apply unless a state-specific endorsement provides otherwise.

Payroll records, job duties, certificates, and subcontractor information must be retained for rating verification.

No notice, inspection, or audit changes coverage unless an endorsement is issued and attached to the policy.

References to classification, remuneration, and rating basis include VT class code 5606 only for the state and operation shown in the information page.

Headings are included for ease of reading and do not alter statutory benefits, employers liability limits, audit rights, or state amendatory provisions.

If a state endorsement and a general condition address the same subject, the state-specific endorsement controls for the affected state.

The insured should retain payroll journals, tax filings, subcontractor certificates, job-duty records, and officer status records used to support the classification entries.

Classification summaries on one page do not replace the information page, payroll schedule, endorsement schedule, or premium audit statement.

A certificate, binder note, invoice, or producer correspondence item does not amend a payroll or class-code entry unless an endorsement is issued.

Final premium may require allocation of remuneration by state, governing class, officer status, overtime treatment, and subcontracted work records.

When a class code appears on multiple schedules, the state, item identifier, and effective date should be used to read the entries together.

**SECTION A - RECORDS AND AUDIT**

The insured must keep payroll journals, tax filings, job-duty records, and contract labor records for Contractor executive supervisor assigned to class code 5606 in VT.

The remuneration entry of $223,415 is an estimate for rating purposes and may be revised after audit without changing the coverage afforded by the policy.

Separate records are required when an employee performs duties that may fall under more than one classification or more than one covered state.

If adequate records are not available, remuneration may be assigned to the highest rated applicable classification permitted by the rating rules.

**SECTION B - STATE AND CLASSIFICATION CONDITIONS**

State amendatory endorsements, statutory benefit provisions, and assigned-risk rules apply before any conflicting general condition in this policy packet.

A classification shown on a schedule is not a warranty that all operations at the insured location are limited to that class.

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Authorized Representative                                            Countersignature Date
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Blue Kettle Food Service, LLC                                                                               WC 00 00 01 A

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
                                           POLICY CHANGE ENDORSEMENT

Endorsement No. WC-EN-033                                                                    Effective 09/01/2026

"ITEM","STATE / CLASS"
"WC-0033","CT / 8810"
"CLASSIFICATION","PAYROLL / RATE"
"Clerical office employees","$416,547 / 1.15"
"PREMIUM","FORM"
"$4,790","WC 00 00 00 C 04 21"
"ENDORSEMENT","EFFECTIVE DATE"
"WC-EN-033","09/01/2026"
"MATERIALITY",""
"Administrative",""

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

POLICY CONDITIONS
This page applies to classification 8810 in CT as shown in the information page and classification schedule.

Estimated remuneration, class assignments, rates, and premium are subject to audit after the policy period.

The experience modification factor and schedule rating entry apply unless a state-specific endorsement provides otherwise.

Payroll records, job duties, certificates, and subcontractor information must be retained for rating verification.

No notice, inspection, or audit changes coverage unless an endorsement is issued and attached to the policy.

References to classification, remuneration, and rating basis include CT class code 8810 only for the state and operation shown in the information page.

Headings are included for ease of reading and do not alter statutory benefits, employers liability limits, audit rights, or state amendatory provisions.

If a state endorsement and a general condition address the same subject, the state-specific endorsement controls for the affected state.

The insured should retain payroll journals, tax filings, subcontractor certificates, job-duty records, and officer status records used to support the classification entries.

Classification summaries on one page do not replace the information page, payroll schedule, endorsement schedule, or premium audit statement.


A certificate, binder note, invoice, or producer correspondence item does not amend a payroll or class-code entry unless an endorsement is issued.

Final premium may require allocation of remuneration by state, governing class, officer status, overtime treatment, and subcontracted work records.

When a class code appears on multiple schedules, the state, item identifier, and effective date should be used to read the entries together.

SECTION A - RECORDS AND AUDIT
The insured must keep payroll journals, tax filings, job-duty records, and contract labor records for Clerical office employees assigned to class code 8810 in CT.

The remuneration entry of $416,547 is an estimate for rating purposes and may be revised after audit without changing the coverage afforded by the policy.

Separate records are required when an employee performs duties that may fall under more than one classification or more than one covered state.

If adequate records are not available, remuneration may be assigned to the highest rated applicable classification permitted by the rating rules.

SECTION B - STATE AND CLASSIFICATION CONDITIONS
State amendatory endorsements, statutory benefit provisions, and assigned-risk rules apply before any conflicting general condition in this policy packet.

A classification shown on a schedule is not a warranty that all operations at the insured location are limited to that class.

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Authorized Representative                                                   Countersignature Date
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Blue Kettle Food Service, LLC                                                                        WC 00 00 00 C

# Page 162

ARGENT BIRCH EMPLOYERS | WORKERS COMPENSATION AND EMPLOYERS LIABILITY
### Policy Change Endorsement 27

                                                                    YW700400
                                                     04/01/2026 - 04/01/2027

---

# POLICY CHANGE ENDORSEMENT

Endorsement No. WC-EN-053                                  Effective 05/01/2026

ITEM,STATE / CLASS
WC-0053,RI / 9082
CLASSIFICATION,PAYROLL / RATE
Restaurant NOC,$642,370 / 4.35
PREMIUM,FORM
$27,943,WC 00 00 01 A 01 15
ENDORSEMENT,EFFECTIVE DATE
WC-EN-053,05/01/2026
MATERIALITY,
No Material Change,

---

### POLICY CONDITIONS

This page applies to classification 9082 in RI as shown in the information page and classification schedule.

Estimated remuneration, class assignments, rates, and premium are subject to audit after the policy period.

The experience modification factor and schedule rating entry apply unless a state-specific endorsement provides otherwise.

Payroll records, job duties, certificates, and subcontractor information must be retained for rating verification.

No notice, inspection, or audit changes coverage unless an endorsement is issued and attached to the policy.

References to classification, remuneration, and rating basis include RI class code 9082 only for the state and operation shown in the information page.

Headings are included for ease of reading and do not alter statutory benefits, employers liability limits, audit rights, or state amendatory provisions.

If a state endorsement and a general condition address the same subject, the state-specific endorsement controls for the affected state.

The insured should retain payroll journals, tax filings, subcontractor certificates, job-duty records, and officer status records used to support the classification entries.

Classification summaries on one page do not replace the information page, payroll schedule, endorsement schedule, or premium audit statement.

---

A certificate, binder note, invoice, or producer correspondence item does not amend a payroll or class-code entry unless an endorsement is issued.

Final premium may require allocation of remuneration by state, governing class, officer status, overtime treatment, and subcontracted work records.

When a class code appears on multiple schedules, the state, item identifier, and effective date should be used to read the entries together.

#### SECTION A - RECORDS AND AUDIT

The insured must keep payroll journals, tax filings, job-duty records, and contract labor records for Restaurant NOC assigned to class code 9082 in RI.

The remuneration entry of $642,370 is an estimate for rating purposes and may be revised after audit without changing the coverage afforded by the policy.

Separate records are required when an employee performs duties that may fall under more than one classification or more than one covered state.

If adequate records are not available, remuneration may be assigned to the highest rated applicable classification permitted by the rating rules.

#### SECTION B - STATE AND CLASSIFICATION CONDITIONS

State amendatory endorsements, statutory benefit provisions, and assigned-risk rules apply before any conflicting general condition in this policy packet.

A classification shown on a schedule is not a warranty that all operations at the insured location are limited to that class.

---

__________________________________            __________________________________
Authorized Representative                     Countersignature Date

---

Blue Kettle Food Service, LLC                                      WC 00 00 01 A

**POLICY CONDITIONS**

This page applies to classification 8810 in CT as shown in the information page and classification schedule.

Estimated remuneration, class assignments, rates, and premium are subject to audit after the policy period.

The experience modification factor and schedule rating entry apply unless a state-specific endorsement provides otherwise.

Payroll records, job duties, certificates, and subcontractor information must be retained for rating verification.

No notice, inspection, or audit changes coverage unless an endorsement is issued and attached to the policy.

References to classification, remuneration, and rating basis include CT class code 8810 only for the state and operation shown in the information page.

Headings are included for ease of reading and do not alter statutory benefits, employers liability limits, audit rights, or state amendatory provisions.

If a state endorsement and a general condition address the same subject, the state-specific endorsement controls for the affected state.

The insured should retain payroll journals, tax filings, subcontractor certificates, job-duty records, and officer status records used to support the classification entries.

Classification summaries on one page do not replace the information page, payroll schedule, endorsement schedule, or premium audit statement.

---

A certificate, binder note, invoice, or producer correspondence item does not amend a payroll or class-code entry unless an endorsement is issued.

Final premium may require allocation of remuneration by state, governing class, officer status, overtime treatment, and subcontracted work records.

When a class code appears on multiple schedules, the state, item identifier, and effective date should be used to read the entries together.

**SECTION A - RECORDS AND AUDIT**

The insured must keep payroll journals, tax filings, job-duty records, and contract labor records for Clerical office employees assigned to class code 8810 in CT.

The remuneration entry of $502,147 is an estimate for rating purposes and may be revised after audit without changing the coverage afforded by the policy.

Separate records are required when an employee performs duties that may fall under more than one classification or more than one covered state.

If adequate records are not available, remuneration may be assigned to the highest rated applicable classification permitted by the rating rules.

**SECTION B - STATE AND CLASSIFICATION CONDITIONS**

State amendatory endorsements, statutory benefit provisions, and assigned-risk rules apply before any conflicting general condition in this policy packet.

A classification shown on a schedule is not a warranty that all operations at the insured location are limited to that class.

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

POLICY CONDITIONS

This page applies to classification 8742 in MA as shown in the information page and classification schedule.

Estimated remuneration, class assignments, rates, and premium are subject to audit after the policy period.

The experience modification factor and schedule rating entry apply unless a state-specific endorsement provides otherwise.

Payroll records, job duties, certificates, and subcontractor information must be retained for rating verification.

No notice, inspection, or audit changes coverage unless an endorsement is issued and attached to the policy.

References to classification, remuneration, and rating basis include MA class code 8742 only for the state and operation shown in the information page.

Headings are included for ease of reading and do not alter statutory benefits, employers liability limits, audit rights, or state amendatory provisions.

If a state endorsement and a general condition address the same subject, the state-specific endorsement controls for the affected state.

The insured should retain payroll journals, tax filings, subcontractor certificates, job-duty records, and officer status records used to support the classification entries.

Classification summaries on one page do not replace the information page, payroll schedule, endorsement schedule, or premium audit statement.

---

A certificate, binder note, invoice, or producer correspondence item does not amend a payroll or class-code entry unless an endorsement is issued.

Final premium may require allocation of remuneration by state, governing class, officer status, overtime treatment, and subcontracted work records.

When a class code appears on multiple schedules, the state, item identifier, and effective date should be used to read the entries together.

SECTION A - RECORDS AND AUDIT

The insured must keep payroll journals, tax filings, job-duty records, and contract labor records for Outside salespersons assigned to class code 8742 in MA.

The remuneration entry of $622,528 is an estimate for rating purposes and may be revised after audit without changing the coverage afforded by the policy.

Separate records are required when an employee performs duties that may fall under more than one classification or more than one covered state.

If adequate records are not available, remuneration may be assigned to the highest rated applicable classification permitted by the rating rules.

SECTION B - STATE AND CLASSIFICATION CONDITIONS

State amendatory endorsements, statutory benefit provisions, and assigned-risk rules apply before any conflicting general condition in this policy packet.

A classification shown on a schedule is not a warranty that all operations at the insured location are limited to that class.
